***злоба.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:злоба.html>зло́ба</a> (3984)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">зълоба</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zŭloba</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*zъloba</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*zъlъ</i> + |  <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-oba</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:злой.html>злой</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zloj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-оба</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-oba</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:злоба.html>зло́ба</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zlóba</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:злоба.html>зло́бы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:злоба.html>зло́бы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:злоба.html>зло́б</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>spite, malice</li>
<li>rage, anger
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кипеть.html>кипе́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:злоба.html>зло́бой</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kipétʹ <b>zlóboj</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to boil <b>with anger</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>grudge</li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:злой.html>злой</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zloj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:злой.html>зло</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zlo</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">evil</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вонь.html>вонь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vonʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stench</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ие</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зловоние.html>злово́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zlovónije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зловоние.html>злово́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зловоние.html>злово́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зловоние.html>злово́ний</a></b>)

***зловонный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зловонный.html>злово́нный</a> (15445)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зловоние.html>злово́ние</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zlovónije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:злой.html>зло</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zlo</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">evil</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вонь.html>вонь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vonʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stench</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зловонный.html>злово́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zlovónnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)злово́ннее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)злово́нней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fetid, smelly, foul-smelling</li></ol>

***злодей.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:злодей.html>злоде́й</a> (6940)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:злой.html>зло</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zlo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-дей</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-dej</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, combining form of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">де́ять</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">déjatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to do</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:злодей.html>злоде́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zlodéj</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:злодей.html>злоде́я</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:злодей.html>злоде́и</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:злодей.html>злоде́ев</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:злодейка.html>злоде́йка</a></b>)

***злой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:злой.html>злой</a> (1292)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*zъlъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:злой.html>злой</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zloj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)зле́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)зле́й</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:злейший.html>зле́йший</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>wicked, evil, ill-natured
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:злой.html>злы́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>дела́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zlýje</b> delá</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>evil</b> deeds</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>malicious, malevolent, spiteful
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:губа.html>гу́бы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:искривить.html>искриви́ла</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:злой.html>зла́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:улыбка.html>улы́бка</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jevó gúby iskrivíla <b>zlája</b> ulýbka.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">A <b>malevolent</b> smile played on his lips.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>angry, enraged
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осторожно.html>осторо́жно</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:злой.html>зла́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:собака.html>соба́ка</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ostoróžno, <b>zlája</b> sobáka!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Beware of <b>angry</b> dog.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>rabid, irate, venomous</li>
<li>fierce, severe, bitter
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:злой.html>злой</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ветер.html>ве́тер</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zloj</b> véter</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a <b>bitter</b> wind</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>ill, harmful, evil, bad
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:злой.html>зла́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:судьба.html>судьба́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zlája</b> sudʹbá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">an <b>ill</b> fate</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> pungent, stinging, painfully spicy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:злой.html>зла́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:приправа.html>припра́ва</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zlája</b> pripráva</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a <b>pungent</b> seasoning</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> malignant</li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:злой.html>зло</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zlo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:злой.html>зло</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zlo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:качество.html>ка́чество</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">káčestvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-енный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:злокачественный.html>злока́чественный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zlokáčestvennyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)злока́чественнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)злока́чественней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> malignant <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">tending to cause death</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:злокачественный.html>злока́чественная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:опухоль.html>о́пухоль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zlokáčestvennaja</b> ópuxolʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">malignant tumor</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доброкачественный.html>доброка́чественный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dobrokáčestvennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> malignant, malevolent</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> immoral</li></ol>

***злопамятный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:злопамятный.html>злопа́мятный</a> (27181)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:злой.html>зло</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zlo</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">evil</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:память.html>па́мять</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pámjatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">memory</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:злопамятный.html>злопа́мятный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zlopámjatnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)злопа́мятнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)злопа́мятней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>vindictive, rancorous, unforgiving, likely to hold a grudge</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<table style="float:right; clear:right; margin-left:0.5em; margin-bottom:0.5em; border: 1px solid 6699CC; border-collapse:collapse;" cellpadding="2" rules="all" width="210" class="morfotable ru">
<tbody><tr>

<th bgcolor="EEF9FF" colspan="3" align="center"> ед. ч.</th>
<th bgcolor="EEF9FF" rowspan="2" align="center" style="vertical-align:center;"> мн. ч.</th>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:злорадно.html>злора́дно</a> (12966)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:злорадный.html>злора́дный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zlorádnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:злорадно.html>злора́дно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zlorádno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>gloatingly</li>
<li>spitefully, malevolently</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:злостный.html>зло́стный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zlóstnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>malicious
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:злостный.html>зло́стная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:клевета.html>клевета́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zlóstnaja</b> klevetá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">malicious slander</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>fraudulent
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:злостный.html>зло́стное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:банкротство.html>банкро́тство</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zlóstnoje</b> bankrótstvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">fraudulent bankruptcy</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>persistent <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">offender</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:злостный.html>зло́стный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:неплательщик.html>неплате́льщик</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zlóstnyj</b> neplatélʹščik</i> ― <span class="e-translation">persistent non-payer/defaulter</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">malicious</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:злобный.html>зло́бный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zlóbnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:злой.html>злой</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zloj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:злость.html>злость</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zlostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:злость.html>зло́сти</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:злость.html>зло́сти</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:злость.html>зло́стей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>spite, malice, rage, anger, grudge <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a strong feeling of displeasure, hostility or antagonism towards someone or something</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">злоупотреби́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zloupotrebítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:змеиный.html>змеи́ный</a> (10280)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:змея.html>змея́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zmejá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ínyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:змеиный.html>змеи́ный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zmeínyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> snake; serpentine
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:змеиный.html>змеи́ный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:укус.html>уку́с</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zmeínyj</b> ukús</i> ― <span class="e-translation">bite of a snake; snakebite</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:змеиный.html>змеи́ная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кожа.html>ко́жа</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zmeínaja</b> kóža</i> ― <span class="e-translation">snakeskin</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:змеиный.html>змеи́ное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гнездо.html>гнездо́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zmeínoje gnezdó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">nest of vipers</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> serpentine, venomous, viperine</li></ol>

***змей.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:змея.html>змей</a> (4611)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*zmьjь</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:змий.html>змий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zmij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a borrowing from Old Church Slavonic.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:змея.html>змей</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zmej</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:змея.html>зме́я</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:змея.html>зме́и</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:змей.html>зме́ев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mythology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> serpent, dragon</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> snake <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">crafty, wily, evil man</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>kite <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">flying toy</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms_2">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воздушный.html>возду́шный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:змея.html>змей</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vozdúšnyj zmej</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зеленый.html>зелёный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:змий.html>змий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zeljónyj zmij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:змея.html>змей</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zmej</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">genitive plural of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:змея.html>змея́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zmejá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">accusative plural of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:змея.html>змея́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zmejá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p>Diminutive of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:змея.html>змея́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zmejá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:змейка.html>зме́йка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zméjka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:змейка.html>зме́йки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:змейка.html>зме́йки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:змейка.html>зме́ек</a></b>)

***змея.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:змея.html>змея</a> (3098)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*zmьja</i>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:змея.html>змея́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zmejá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:змея.html>змеи́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:змея.html>зме́и</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:змея.html>змей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>snake, serpent</li>
<li>crafty, sneaky person, snake</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

***змий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:змий.html>змий</a> (27865)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu"><a href = vnd.unilang:змий.html>зми́и</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zmii</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*zmь̀jь</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:змея.html>змей</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zmej</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the inherited East Slavic form.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:змий.html>змий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zmij</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:змий.html>зми́я</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:змий.html>зми́и</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:змий.html>зми́ев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mythology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> dragon</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Christianity</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> serpent</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> insidious, cunning, evil man</li></ol>

***знавать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:знавать.html>знава́ть</a> (23192)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>знать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">znatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знавать.html>знава́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">znavátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> usually negative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to experience (joy, grief, defeat, rest, etc.) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">repeatedly or frequently</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>; <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/iterative_aspect" class="extiw" title="w:iterative aspect">iterative</a> of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>знать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">znatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>This is an iterative verb, and in standard language is conjugated only in the infinitive and the past tense.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***знак.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:знак.html>знак</a> (967)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">знакъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">znakŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*znakъ</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*znati</i> + |  <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-kъ</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знак.html>знак</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">znak</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знак.html>зна́ка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знак.html>зна́ки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знак.html>зна́ков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sign, mark
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:знак.html>зна́ки</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:препинание.html>препина́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>znáki</b> prepinánija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">punctuation marks</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:знак.html>знак</a></strong> <a href = vnd.unilang:слабость.html>сла́бости</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v znak slábosti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">as a sign of weakness</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>symbol</li>
<li>omen</li>
<li>badge</li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:твердый.html>твёрдый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знак.html>знак</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">tvjórdyj znak</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мягкий.html>мя́гкий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знак.html>зна́к</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">mjáxkij znák</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знаковый.html>зна́ковый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">znákovyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational<span class="ib-comma">,</span> mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sign
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:знаковый.html>зна́ковый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:разряд.html>разря́д</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>znákovyj</b> razrjád</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>sign</b> digit/position</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:знаковый.html>зна́ковый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:битый.html>бит</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>znákovyj</b> bit</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>sign</b> bit</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:знаковый.html>зна́ковая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:система.html>систе́ма</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>znákovaja</b> sistéma</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/sign_system" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:sign system"><b>sign</b> system</a></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational<span class="ib-comma">,</span> computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> character</li>
<li>token, emblematic, symbolic, indicative</li></ol>
